country_event = { #The Situation of the French Republic - History
	id = nfa.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.1"}
	title = nfa.1.t
	desc = nfa.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_NFA_Early1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.1.a #Political Situation
		NFA = {
			country_event = {
				id = nfa.2
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.5"}

		name = nfa.5.a #Time to return home
		NFA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = committed_to_return_home
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = committed_to_return_home
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NFA = {
				country_event = {
					id = natfra.6 days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = nfa.438
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.438 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = nfa.438.t
	desc = nfa.438.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_flavor37

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = NFA_la_liberation }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.438 days = 355 } # Repeat Eid event
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.438.a #Eid Mubarak!
		add_political_power = 5
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to check if post-war events can fire, depending on owned states and months
	id = nfa.529
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.529 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 762 #Nice
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.518 days = 8 random = 48 } #Restoration of Monaco
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 21 #Marseille
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.8.29
						date < 1939.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.8.29
						date < 1940.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.8.29
						date < 1941.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.8.29
						date < 1942.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.8.29
						date < 1943.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.8.29
						date < 1944.10.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.530 days = 2 } #Festival d'Avignon
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.179 days = 95 } #The question of Montmartre
			country_event = { id = nfa.531 days = 450 } #A mosque in Paris?
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.6.29
						date < 1939.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.6.29
						date < 1940.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.6.29
						date < 1941.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.6.29
						date < 1942.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.6.29
						date < 1943.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.6.29
						date < 1944.8.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.532 days = 2 } #First New Tour de France
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.1.29
						date < 1939.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.1.29
						date < 1940.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.1.29
						date < 1941.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.1.29
						date < 1942.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.1.29
						date < 1943.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.1.29
						date < 1944.2.25
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.540 days = 2 } #Emmaus
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 15 #Normandy
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.533 days = 160 } #Rouen Reconstruction
			country_event = { id = nfa.534 days = 250 } #Tank in Vimoutiers
		}
		country_event = { id = nfa.529 days = 45 } #Loop the event without jumping over months
	}
}

			}
		}

					owns_state = 18
					owns_state = 15

					owns_state = 785
					owns_state = 32
					owns_state = 735
					owns_state = 762
					owns_state = 984
					owns_state = 983
				}
			}
            set_country_flag = NFA_liberated_all_of_france

		if = {
			limit = { 
				owns_state = 20
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 21 
					owns_state = 19
					owns_state = 16
				}
			}
            set_capital = { state = 20 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				owns_state = 21
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 19
					owns_state = 20
				}
			}
             set_capital = { state = 21 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				owns_state = 19

					owns_state = 20
				}
			}
            set_capital = { state = 19 }

			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.13
		}

					owns_state = 16

				}
			}

			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = NFA_mainland_totalist_party_long
				name = NFA_mainland_totalist_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = NFA_mainland_syndicalist_party_long
				name = NFA_mainland_syndicalist_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = NFA_mainland_radical_socialist_party_long
				name = NFA_mainland_radical_socialist_party
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Marcel Cachin"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/FRA/Portrait_France_Marcel_Cachin.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authcom_subtype
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Marie Jeanne Picqueray"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/FRA/Portrait_France_May_Picqueray.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = feminist_syndicalist_subtype
			}
			
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Léon Blum"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/FRA/Portrait_FRA_Leon_Blum_KX.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "National French Loyalists" }
				set_division_template_lock = {
					division_template = "National French Loyalists"
					is_locked = no
				}
			}

			set_variable = { NFA_syndie_resistance_level = 15 }	

		}
	}
}

country_event = { #syndie resistance 1
	id = natfra.132
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event natfra.132"}
	title = natfra.132.t
	desc = natfra.132.d
	picture = GFX_event_NFA_resistance

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			var = NFA_syndie_resistance_level
			value = 14
			compare = greater_than
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = { #ebin
		name = natfra.132.a 
		add_political_power = -20
		add_stability = -0.03
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = NFA_syndie_resistance_2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_syndie_resistance_1
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NFA_syndie_resistance_2 
				add_idea = NFA_syndie_resistance_1
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #ok
		name = natfra.283.a 
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Pierre Marcilhacy"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NFA/Portrait_NFA_Pierre_Marcilhacy.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 800
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 800 }
				retire = yes
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NFR
	}
}

# Rail Fix #
state_event = { #Hidden Event to turn sabotaged railways back on
	id = nfa.88
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.88" }
	title = nfa.88.t
	desc = nfa.88.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes #makes sure the event stays hidden

	option = {
		name = nfa.88.a #Report if seen
		PREV = { #Scope to the state that the rails were sabotaged in
			add_state_modifier = { modifier = { disable_strategic_redeployment = -1 } } #A modifier of -1 turns strategic redeployment back on
			add_state_modifier = { modifier = { local_supplies_for_controller = 0.5 } }	#Turn the supplies back to normal
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The death of Jean III
	id = nfa.310
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.310 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = nfa.310.t
	desc = {
		text = nfa.310.d.noreconquest
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				#No Major French city is back in our hands
				16 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				19 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				20 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				21 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.310.d.reconquest
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				#One Major French city is back in our hands
				16 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				19 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				20 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				21 = {
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_AFFlavorDeathJean

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		has_country_leader = { name = "Jean III" ruling_only = yes }
		date > 1940.6.27
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.310.a #The king is dead, long live the king
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.311 days = 30 }
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Henri VI"
			desc = "POLITICS_HENRI_VI_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NFA/Portrait_NFA_Henri_VI_Drip.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"

			traits = { NFA_Young_Prince }

			name = "Henri VI"

			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = junta_subtype
			traits = { NFA_Young_Prince }
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Henri VI"
			desc = "POLITICS_HENRI_VI_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/NFA/Henri_VI_No_Hat.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = authdem_junta_subtype
			traits = { NFA_Young_Prince }
		}

# French Guinea and Upper Volta

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - French Guinea
	id = nfa.443
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.443"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			806 = { #Guinea
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			808 = { #Upper Volta
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF }
	}

	option = { #Mission Attacked - 444
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Guinea
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.34
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
		country_event = nfa.444
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Volta kings dispute - 471
		trigger = {
			808 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
				808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Upper Volta
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.125
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
		country_event = nfa.471
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Infrastructure Sabotaged - 445
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Upper Volta
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.445
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 144 random = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #Garrison Attacked - 446
		trigger = {
			808 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Upper Volta
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.446
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 216 random = 96 } #loop
	}
	option = { #no effect
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.16
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.83
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				has_country_flag = nfa_volta_kingdoms_dispute
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = nfa.443 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}
}

		}

# Senegal

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - Senegal
	id = nfa.467
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.467"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
			has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = nfa.467 days = 158 random = 36 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Miner strike - 468
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
		country_event = nfa.468
	}

	option = { #Resentment spreading to Lower classes - 469
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 22
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.14
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
		country_event = nfa.469
	}

	option = { #Evolués support the idea of independence - 470
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 12
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
		country_event = nfa.470
	}

	option = { #Nothing happens
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.08
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.42

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - Niger and Wadai
	id = nfa.475
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.475"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			809 = { #Niger
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			515 = { #Chad
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF }
	}

	option = { #The prophet of Iriba - 476
		trigger = {
			515 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			911 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_mad_prophet_chad
				515 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Chad
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 42
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_mad_prophet_chad
		country_event = nfa.476
		country_event = { id = nfa.475 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Clash between bedouins and the army in Niger - 477
		trigger = {
			809 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			910 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 809 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Niger
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 16
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				has_country_flag = nfa_mad_prophet_chad
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.477
		country_event = { id = nfa.475 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Assassination in Chad! - 478
		trigger = {
			515 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			911 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 515 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Chad
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 8
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_mad_prophet_chad
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.478
		country_event = { id = nfa.475 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Bedouins attack a patrol Niger - 479
		trigger = {
			809 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			910 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = { 809 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } #Niger
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 17
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.59
				has_country_flag = nfa_mad_prophet_chad
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.479
		country_event = { id = nfa.475 days = 158 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Nothing happens
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 17

				factor = 1.94
				has_country_flag = nfa_mad_prophet_chad
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = nfa.475 days = 108 random = 96 } #loop
	}
}

country_event = { ###### TUN Revolt
	id = revoltfra.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico_req.591"}
	title = revoltfra.1.t
	desc = revoltfra.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mormons
	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = NFA_french_union
				has_completed_focus = NFA_pacify_algeria
			}
		}
		513 = {
			resistance > 60
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = NFA
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	

	option = { ####YAY
		name = revoltfra.1.a
		activate_mission = NFA_retake_tun_mission
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUN
					is_owned_by = NFA
				}
				TUN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUN = {
			load_oob = TUN_revolt
			declare_war_on = {	
				target = NFA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		}
	}
	option = { ####prevent
		name = revoltfra.1.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = TUN_chance
			}
		}
	custom_effect_tooltip = "Due to our limited resources, we are only able to suppress revolts once!"
		513 = {
			add_resistance = -15
		}
		set_country_flag = TUN_chance
	
	}
}

country_event = { #Collapse of National France if killed or someone got algeria
	id = nfa.623
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.623" }
	title = nfa.623.t
	desc = nfa.623.d

	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		OR = {
			has_capitulated = yes
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 460
				controls_state = 459
				controls_state = 805
				controls_state = 458
			}
		}
		NOT = { #One Major French city is back in our hands
			16 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			19 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			20 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			21 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	
	option = {
		name = nfa.623.a
		
		### Morocco
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = MOR
				}
				country_exists = MOR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 290 #Rif
						state = 699 #Rio de Oro
						state = 968 #Ifni
					}
				}
				MOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		### Kill off NFA
		force_capitulate = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Collapse of National France caused by native revolts with no other invaders
	id = nfa.624
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.624" }
	title = nfa.624.t
	desc = nfa.624.d

	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		OR = {
			has_war_with = TUN

			}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #general
		name = flavorfra.34.a #

			name = "Henri Mordacq"

			}
		}

		}
		if = {

				tag = MSF
			}
			set_global_flag = MSF_MORDACQ
		}

country_event = { #	Mordacq event chain
	id = flavorfra.35
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event flavorfra.35"}
	title = flavorfra.35.t
	desc = flavorfra.35.d
	picture = GFX_event_NFA_mordacq_mudered
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #guarantee
		name = flavorfra.35.a #
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = LPD_MORDACQ
			}
			give_guarantee = LPD
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MSF_MORDACQ
			}
			give_guarantee = MSF
		}
	}
	
	option = { #faction
		name = flavorfra.35.a #
		trigger = {
			LPD = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			MSF = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = LPD_MORDACQ
			}
			ENT = {
				add_to_faction = LPD
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MSF_MORDACQ
			}
			ENT = {
				add_to_faction = MSF
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Economy
		name = flavorfra.35.a #
	
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}	
				
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = LPD_MORDACQ
			}
			LPD = {
				random_owned_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MSF_MORDACQ
			}
			MSF = {
				random_owned_state = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
}
